< text>
Let me start off by saying I have never in my life felt so disrespected and humiliated. My only fault was being a loyal customer for the last 8 months, spending at minimum $50 dollars a week on "icecream", receiving multiple unlimited cups for enormous amount of frozen yogurts I consume and provide for my study group students. The store manager named Aaron was extremely disrespectful and rude beyond belief. I have never taken the time to write a negative review about a business or about anybody, but this was necessary. I will never ever walk in to this store ever again and I will make sure anybody that I know will not as well because of a rude young man who has a title of store manager and behaves in such a disrespectful way, being a "perfect" example for other workers. You guys seriously need to re-evaluate who you hire and more importantly who you hire as managers to lead by example. Upon my observation throughout the months of visiting, he would always (10/10 times) hide behind utility room (I'm really curious what he is always doing back there during his working hours) and when I make noises from the machines he would slowly walkout as if I'm an invisible person. That is completely okay and I don't mind that anymore. I am not a person patronizing workers by requiring them to greet me. But as I walked out of the door strenuously carrying multiple cups of icecream as usual, he shouted at my back, "WELCOME!" thinking I'll leave without even saying thank you. I guess he thinks customers have the obligation to act certain ways but he doesn't. Moreover, he talks to everyone in such a patronizing way, its so hard to describe and extremely difficult to hear. Botton line, I quit going to frozen yogurt and most certainly to this location where Aaron works. Aaron does not deserve to have this job and more importantly does not deserve to have a job as a general manager.
Thank you so much for taking your precious time to read my review.< /text>

I arrived at 5:45 because I heard people arrive hours early at CA DMVs. I was the only one there. People didnâ€™t start showing up until around 7:15. Around 7:45 a DMV employee went down the line asking everyone why they were there and checked for correct documentation. < Review>
Organized and operates with decent efficiency. Staff are friendly enough, but keep in mind they are dealing with hundreds of people a day. Patience is a must. It's like sitting in rush hour traffic. If you don't have an appointment, expect to be here about 2 hours or so. If you don't have an appointment, it is best to either get here more than 30 minutes before they open, or around 2pm in the afternoon.

If you have an appointment, you just need to check in, you don't have to wait in line. They don't explain this very well and it would be helpful if they had some signage that says this.

Driving tests are done by appointment only. If you can't get an appointment here, and the rest of the Bay area is booked, try somewhere further south, such as Capitola.<//Review>

< Text>
I took my beautiful 2 year old rottweiller with a vomiting issue to this place. They wanted to keep her overnight to put her on antibiotics (she had milk in her boobs and no pups because she just had a period... the milk was infected, duhh)  and take care of her.I paid up front and trusted them with my beautiful rottweiller. She was exited and lively, she was just throwing up a couple days. Later that evening she was anxious the vets told us when we called after hours.The next morning they called to tell me she DIED!!  The owner of the clinic argued with me telling me she got septic and died overnight, with IV antibiotics in her. It takes more than just a few hours to kill a anxious and energetic  2 year old rottie with a septic infection. My heart is so pained and the vets won't even admit what they did. I would bet everything on the fact they sedated her and her airway collapsed. This is common when big dogs get sedated. I know she was anxious and I know she cries (howls) when she is separated from her family. To top it all off the owner was rude beyond belief, even insulting me a couple times. So not only was my companion ignorantly killed, the owner insulted me to boot. All this cost over $900 for them to do to our family.
PLEASE do not take your animals to these vets, take it from my broken heart.
Please do not put your animals in the hands of incompitent vets.</Text>
